3. Did you feel like the training content was relevant to your job and helped you perform better?
4. Were the training materials and methods easy to understand and apply?

6. Did you feel like the training duration was sufficient, or did you think it was too short or too long?
7. Did you face any obstacles or challenges while attending the training, and if yes, were they addressed properly?
8. How would you rate the trainer's knowledge and delivery skills?
9. Did the training program provide you with the skills and knowledge necessary to perform your job effectively?
10. Would you recommend this training program to your colleagues?

- If not, which benefits would you like to see?

- Which specific benefits do you value most and why?
- Have you ever had to cancel or postpone a medical procedure because of lack of insurance coverage?

- How important is it for you to have a comprehensive benefits package?

5. **Inclusivity**
- Do you feel that the current benefits package is inclusive and caters to all employees?

- Do you feel that the benefits package is competitive compared to other companies in the industry?

7. **Communication about benefits**
- How satisfied are you with the communication about benefits and the ease of use?
- Are there any specific benefits that you think should be prioritized for the package?

8. **Assistance program**

[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure, I can help you generate a questionnaire on career development. Here are some questions that can be used to gauge an employee's thoughts and feelings about their career development within the company:

1. How long have you been working in this company?
2. What is your current role and how do you feel about it?
3. Do you feel like you have the opportunity to grow and develop within the company?
4. Have you received any training or education to help you perform your job better?
5. How satisfied are you with the career development opportunities available to you in this company?
6. Do you feel like your skills and talents are being fully utilized?
7. Have you been able to achieve your career goals within the company?
8. What steps can the company take to help you achieve your career goals?
9. Do you feel like you have a clear path for career advancement within the company?
10. How often do you receive feedback about your performance and is it specific enough to help you improve?
11. How satisfied are you with the training and development programs offered by the company?
12. Do you feel like your goals and aspirations are in alignment with the company's goals?
13. Have you been able to maintain a healthy work-life balance while pursuing your career goals?
14. What can the company do to make you feel more engaged and committed to your career development?
15. Do you feel like the company values your contributions and is invested in your career development?

I hope this questionnaire will be helpful in investigating career development within the company. Let me know if you need it in a specific format.

```json
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Yes"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "No"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q03",

            "TYPE_ID": 3,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Very satisfied"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Somewhat satisfied"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Neutral"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Somewhat dissatisfied"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Very dissatisfied"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q04",
            "NAME": "How often do you receive feedback about your performance and is it specific enough to help you improve?",
            "TYPE_ID": 5,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 4,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": {
                  "ANSWER": "Never",
                  "WEIGHT": 0
                },
                {
                  "ANSWER": "Less than once a year",
                  "WEIGHT": 1
                },
                {
                  "ANSWER": "Once a year",
                  "WEIGHT": 2
                },
                {
                  "ANSWER": "More than once a year",
                  "WEIGHT": 3
                }
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire has 4 questions, each with a unique code and name. The questions are of type "3" which is for rating something. The answers for each question are also defined with a unique code and name. The answers are given a weight based on how often the feedback is received.

1. Do you feel like you have a clear understanding of the different career paths available within the company?
2. Have you ever felt like you are stuck in a dead-end job without any prospects for advancement?
3. How often do you think about your future career goals and how to achieve them?
4. Do you feel like the company provides enough resources and support to help you advance in your career?
5. Do you feel like you have a clear career path within the company, or do you think you might need to look for opportunities outside the company?
6. Have you ever felt like you are not being considered for certain opportunities because of your current position?
7. How often do you discuss career paths and opportunities with your manager?
8. Do you feel like you have to leave the company to advance in your career?
9. Do you feel like you have a good understanding of the skills and qualifications needed to move up in your career?
10. Do you feel like the company provides enough training and development opportunities to help you advance in your career?

This JSON object represents a questionnaire with one questionnaire and six questions. The questions are displayed in order and each question has four possible answers, represented by the `_TF_ANSWERS` field. The `DISPLAY_ORDER` field is used to determine the order in which the questions should be displayed.

3. What types of feedback mechanisms are most effective in promoting continuous improvement?
4. How do you ensure that feedback is collected from a diverse set of stakeholders, including employees, customers, and partners?
5. Can you share some examples of feedback mechanisms that have been particularly successful in driving positive change?
6. How do you measure the effectiveness of feedback mechanisms, and what metrics are used?
7. How do you ensure that feedback is delivered in a constructive and actionable manner?
8. Can you share some best practices for collecting and analyzing feedback in a way that is both efficient and effective?
9. How do you determine the appropriate frequency and volume of feedback to provide, and how do you balance the need for timely feedback with the risk of overwhelming stakeholders?
10. Can you share some lessons learned from implementing feedback mechanisms, including any challenges that were encountered and how they were addressed?

I hope this questionnaire will help you gather the information you need about feedback mechanisms within your company. Let me know if you would like me to convert it into a specific format.
     - User: 
Generate me a questionnaire on Feedback Mechanisms

[LLM ANSWER] -> JSON 
 Here is the questionnaire on Feedback Mechanisms in JSON format, respecting the format you specified:

```json
{
  "data": {
    "TF_QUESTIONNAIRES": [
      {
        "CODE": "FEEDBACK_MECHANISMS",
        "NAME": "Feedback Mechanisms",
        "TYPE_ID": 3,
        "_TF_QUESTIONS": [
          {
            "CODE": "Q01",
            "NAME": "What types of feedback mechanisms are most effective in promoting continuous improvement?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 1,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "Anonymous feedback"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Feedback through a manager"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Feedback through a third party"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "Self-assessment"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q02",
            "NAME": "How do you ensure that feedback is collected from a diverse set of stakeholders, including employees, customers, and partners?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 2,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "By using a variety of methods, including surveys, focus groups, and one-on-one interviews"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "By actively seeking out input from underrepresented groups"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "By providing multiple channels for feedback, including online and offline methods"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "By making the feedback process anonymous"
              }
            ]
          },
          {
            "CODE": "Q03",
            "NAME": "How do you determine the appropriate frequency and volume of feedback to provide, and how do you balance the need for timely feedback with the risk of overwhelming stakeholders?",
            "TYPE_ID": 4,
            "DISPLAY_ORDER": 3,
            "_TF_ANSWERS": [
              {
                "ANSWER": "By using a data-driven approach and setting specific targets for feedback"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "By providing feedback in a timely manner, but not overwhelming stakeholders"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "By balancing the need for timely feedback with the risk of overwhelming stakeholders"
              },
              {
                "ANSWER": "By using a combination of real-time and scheduled feedback"
              }
            ]
          }
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

This questionnaire has three questions, each with four possible answers. The questions are:

1. "What types of feedback mechanisms are most effective in promoting continuous improvement?"
2. "How do you ensure that feedback is collected from a diverse set of stakeholders, including employees, customers, and partners?"
3. "How do you determine the appropriate frequency and volume of feedback to provide, and how do you balance the need for timely feedback with the risk of overwhelming stakeholders?"

The answers provided are:

* Anonymous feedback
* Feedback through a manager
* Feedback through a third party
* Self-assessment
* By using a variety of methods, including surveys, focus groups, and one-on-one interviews
* By actively seeking out input from underrepresented groups
* By providing multiple channels for feedback, including online and offline methods
* By making the feedback process anonymous
* By using a data-driven approach and setting specific targets for feedback
* By providing feedback in a timely manner, but not overwhelming stakeholders
* By balancing the need for timely feedback with the risk of overwhelming stakeholders
* By using a combination of real-time and scheduled feedback

I hope this JSON format meets your requirements. Let me know if you need any further assistance.

 Sure, I can generate a questionnaire on Health and Safety Measures for you. Here are some questions that can be used to assess the health and safety measures of a company:

1. Does your company have a written health and safety policy that is communicated to all employees?
2. Are hazard identification and risk assessment procedures in place to identify and mitigate potential health and safety risks?
3. Are there enough resources, including trained personnel, to implement and maintain health and safety measures?
4. Are there procedures in place to prevent and manage workplace accidents and incidents?
5. Does your company provide adequate training to employees on health and safety procedures?
6. Are there procedures in place to ensure that equipment and machinery are safe and well-maintained?
7. Does your company have a system for reporting and recording health and safety incidents and concerns?
8. Are there procedures in place to ensure that all employees have access to necessary personal protective equipment (PPE)?
9. Does your company have a system for consulting with employees and their representatives on health and safety matters?
10. Does your company collect and analyze data on health and safety performance, and use it to improve performance?
11. Are there procedures in place to ensure that the work environment is safe, including temperature, noise, and lighting levels?
12. Does your company have a system for monitoring and controlling harmful substances, including biological and chemical agents?
13. Does your company have a system for managing stress and psychosocial risks?
14. Are there procedures in place to ensure that employees have adequate facilities, including drinking water, toilets, and eating facilities?
15. Does your company have a system for managing musculoskeletal disorders and other work-related health issues?
16. Does your company have a system for managing the health and safety of remote workers and employees who work from home?
17. Does your company have a system for managing the health and safety of young workers, pregnant workers, and workers with disabilities?
18. Does your company have a system for managing the health and safety of contractors and other non-permanent workers?
19. Does your company have a system for managing the health and safety of visitors, including the general public?
20. Does your company have a system for managing the health and safety of employees who work at heights, in confined spaces, or with dangerous machinery?

This JSON represents a questionnaire with 5 questions, each with a unique code, content, type, display order, and a list of possible answers. The questionnaire code is "HEALTH\_AND\_SAFETY\_MEASURES", and its name is "Health and Safety Measures". Each question is displayed in order, and the type of question is 3, which means it is a rating question. The 5 questions are:

1. "HAZARD\_ID\_RISK\_ASSESSMENT": Are hazard identification and risk assessment procedures in place to identify and mitigate potential health and safety risks?
2. "SAFE\_AND\_WELL\_MAINTAINED": Are there procedures in place to ensure that equipment and machinery are safe and well-maintained?
3. "PERSONAL\_PROTECTIVE\_EQUIPMENT": Are there procedures in place to ensure that all employees have access to necessary personal protective equipment (PPE)?
4. "HAZARD\_REPORTING\_SYSTEM": Is there a system for reporting and recording health and safety incidents and concerns?
5. "HAZARD\_IDENTIFICATION": Does your company have a system for collecting and analyzing data on health and safety performance, and use it to improve performance?

Each question is a rating question, and the answers are "Yes" and "No".

8. Were the communication channels and technology used in the meeting reliable and easy to use?
9. Did you feel that the level of participation and engagement from all meeting attendees was satisfactory?
10. Were the topics discussed in the meeting relevant and important for your work?
11. Did you feel that the meeting was inclusive and that all participants had equal opportunities to contribute?
12. Were the action items and next steps clearly defined and communicated?
13. Did you feel that the meeting was a good use of your time?
14. Do you have any suggestions for improving the kick-off meeting in the future?

3. Were you provided with enough resources and materials to perform your job effectively?
4. Did you feel that the training you received was sufficient and relevant to your role?
5. Were you able to establish a good working relationship with your manager and colleagues?
6. How would you rate the communication and collaboration with your team during the onboarding process?
7. Were there any obstacles or challenges that made your onboarding process difficult?
8. Did you feel that the onboarding process was personalized to your needs and preferences?
9. How would you rate the technology and tools used during the onboarding process?
10. Do you feel that the onboarding process has prepared you for success in your new role?
11. Is there anything specific that you would change about the onboarding process?
12. How well do you feel that your values align with the company culture?
13. Were you provided with a clear understanding of your role and responsibilities?
14. How would you rate the onboarding process in terms of speed and efficiency?
15. Were you able to establish a good work-life balance during the onboarding process?

If the type\_ID is 3, then the answer is a rating. The display order of each question is also specified.

The first question asks about the importance of employees feeling recognized and rewarded, with possible answers being "Not important", "Somewhat important", "Important", and "Very important". The second question asks whether the company has a formal recognition and rewards program in place, with possible answers being "Yes, a formal program is in place" and "No, a formal program is not in place". The third question asks how often employees are recognized and rewarded, with possible answers being "Always", "Most of the time", "Some of the time", and "Never". The ninth question asks about the overall effectiveness of the recognition and rewards program, with possible answers being "Very effective", "Somewhat effective", "Neutral", "Somewhat ineffective", and "Very ineffective".

This questionnaire can be used to gather information about the recognition and rewards program at a company and the perceptions of employees about that program. The data gathered from this questionnaire can be used to improve the recognition and rewards program and make it more effective.

Generate me a questionnaire on Training and Development Programs

-------------------
-------------------
[LLM ANSWER]
 Sure, I can generate a questionnaire on Training and Development Programs for you. Here are some questions that can help you gather information about the effectiveness of such programs:

1. To what extent does the company provide adequate training and development opportunities to its employees?
2. How would you rate the quality of training materials and resources provided by the company?
3. How often do you get training opportunities, and what is the average length of these training sessions?
4. How well do you think the training programs are aligned with the company's goals and values?
5. How satisfied are you with the current training and development programs in terms of content, delivery, and timing?
6. How would you rate the flexibility of the training programs to cater to different learning styles and preferences?
7. How well do you feel the training programs have helped you perform your job better and more efficiently?
8. How satisfied are you with the trainers and their ability to engage and motivate learners?
9. How satisfied are you with the accessibility and convenience of training sessions, in terms of location, time, and frequency?

Each question is presented as a statement, and the respondent is asked to choose one of the 4 possible answers. The answers are presented in a way that makes it easy to calculate a score for each question and then compute an overall score. The scores can be used to classify respondents into different groups, such as those with good or bad work-life balance.

1. How would you describe the physical environment of your workplace? Is it clean, well-lit, and well-maintained?
2. Do you feel comfortable and safe in your workplace?
3. How would you rate the level of noise in your workplace? Is it too loud, too quiet, or just right?
4. Are you satisfied with the temperature in your workplace?
5. How would you rate the level of privacy in your workplace? Do you feel like you have enough privacy, or do you feel like everything is too open?
6. How would you rate the level of collaboration and communication in your workplace? Is it easy to work with others, or do you feel like you are on an island?
7. How would you rate the level of technology and resources available in your workplace? Is it sufficient, or do you feel like you are lacking some tools?
8. How would you rate the level of flexibility in your workplace? Are you able to work from home or adjust your schedule if needed, or do you feel like you are tied to a specific schedule and location?
9. How would you rate the level of support and resources available to you in your workplace? Is it easy to get help if you need it, or do you feel like you are on your own?
10. How would you rate the level of recognition and appreciation you receive in your workplace? Do you feel like your contributions are valued, or do you feel like you are just a number?
